Before every hand, each player has to choose 3 cards and pass them to another player with one exception. For every fourth hand no cards are passed. If you don't have a card of the suit which started the trick you can place any card.\r\n✓ Players can start tricks with a card from any suit, with one exception: the cards of hearts.
